## v1.0.9 — MCP Writeback Byte-Verify + Mac set_theme Persist Closure (session <audit-session>) — DONE

**Reduce date**: 2026-06-05
**Session**: <audit-session>
**Binary**: mac=1db044e8efab (sha12), live IDB AiMaMi.i64, all byte-confirmed against genuine 1.0.9 SOT
**Owner-gate**: EXPLICIT_TAKEOVER ADDITIVE on both surfaces — verified <workstation>/codex mcp bundle (NOT overwritten) + same-owner update of <workstation> windows-1.0.9-ui theme bundle. No canonical overwrite, no raw/intermediate written.

### (A) MCP writeback byte-confirm verification (macos-1.0.9-mcp) — PASS

All 4 mac mcp owner VAs byte-match the genuine 1.0.9 mac IDB; full chain re-verified live:

| command | recorded owner | live IDB owner | size | core delegate | match |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| load_mcp_servers | 0x10015be84 | 0x10015be84 | 0x3c0 | core 0x10061db2c | ✅ |
| upsert_mcp_server | 0x10015c8d4 | 0x10015c8d4 | 0x808 | core 0x10061fcc0 | ✅ |
| set_mcp_server_enabled | 0x10015d360 | 0x10015d360 | 0x518 | core 0x100621f4c | ✅ |
| remove_mcp_server | 0x10015c300 | 0x10015c300 | 0x484 | core 0x10061f5bc | ✅ |

- **fs-write leaf byte-confirmed**: `core::mcp::upsert_mcp_server (0x10061fcc0)` → `save_config_text (0x10061f480)` → `core::relay::atomic_write::write_atomic (0x1006729f8)` → config.toml durable write. Matches queue claim `save_config_text → relay::atomic_write::write_atomic`.
- **DTO** McpServer name/command/args/url/headers/env/enabled byte-confirmed (transport kind switch stdio/http/sse); **McpServerSummary** stride 224B return Vec; **error** CoreError→CoreEnvelope (sentinel 0x8000000000000000); **threading** pure sync mutex/TOML, NO async/spawn for all 4; **block boundary** `insert_mcp_block (0x10061d6dc)` respects `# <<< aimami-relay managed/codex-router` sentinels.
- **Verdict**: writeback PASS. NO fake walls, NO accepted_unknown, NO fabrication. Bundle's own gate `readyToImplement / full_leaf_100=true` is SUPPORTED by binary evidence and is the CORRECT tier — **<workstation> content left intact, not downgraded.**
- **Tier-record discrepancy flagged (not overwritten)**: `AI-EXECUTION-QUEUE.md` line 762-763 (3-Lane Consolidation ACK 2026-06-05) records macos/windows-1.0.9-mcp as `strictImplementationUse (4 cmds)`, but the bundle manifest/gate-report/task-plan/producer-ledger record `readyToImplement / full_leaf_100=true`. Binary evidence supports `readyToImplement`; the consolidation-ACK summary line is a conservative under-record, NOT the canonical tier.

### (B) Mac set_theme persist — genuine_unclosed CLOSED as genuine_no_persist

The 1 `genuine_unclosed` from <audit-session> ("does mac set_theme persist to settings.json like win?") is now resolved:

- **Method**: `xrefs_to AppHandle::set_theme@0x100347e08` → single caller = the inlined window-plugin set_theme command future body `tauri::ipc::InvokeResolver::respond_async_serialized_inner::{{closure}} @0x1000fa294` (the "upper window-plugin closure" the prior pass had not reversed). Full decompile: async-resumed body, complete callee set = `from_command`×2 (extract AppHandle + theme byte @frame+2448) → `AppHandle::set_theme` (send SetTheme code 35 to wry) → `__rust_alloc(128)` building `"null"` (0x6c6c756e) response → `InvokeResolver::return_result`.
- **No-persist proof**: the complete callee set has **NO** `save_config_text`, **NO** `settings_persist_write`, **NO** config.toml/settings.json/fs write. Cross-confirmed by capability table @0x100f379fc (`allow-set-theme`→`set_theme` alongside `allow-set-decorations` etc.) → mac `set_theme` is a pure upstream `@tauri-apps` window-plugin command, **no source archive mac owner** (unlike win source archive owner 0x1408adf90).
- **Fake-wall taxonomy exhausted**: not drop-shim stop (drop shim 0x1000b03c8; real body via AppHandle::set_theme caller xref), not async-bail (full body decompiled), not budget self-limit, not wrong-VA. **Verdict definitive (mac apply-only, no persist), NOT a genuine_ceiling.**
- **source archive impl guidance reaffirmed**: theme = mac apply-only (no settings write on theme change) + win apply+persist (settings.json via 0x1408adf90). `theme_platform_diff` genuine_unclosed list now empty.

**Status**: **done**. Deliverables: THEME-PLATFORM-DIFF-109-DISTILLED.md (Open→Closed) + windows-1.0.9-ui/gate-report.json (genuine_unclosed→closed_findings) + INDEX.jsonl 2 appends (this session) + this section.

## <audit-session> WIN FRONTEND CCF FIRST-PARTY dim1 CLOSURE — 2026-06-05

**Session**: <audit-session>

**Method**: 用第一方 win-PE 前端 CCF dump（INDEX field `win-frontend-ccf-extract` line 1462, machine <workstation>）做 win 后端 28 命令面的 dim1 收口。`AiMaM 1.0.9 win64.exe` = Tauri 单文件 PE32+（SHA a5822387fa3f, base 0x140000000, NOT NSIS）；前端嵌 PE `.rdata`，tauri-dumper 直接对安装包 PE 本体 dump。win 前端 = mac 前端（同一 React/Vite build）：30/30 JS+CSS 字节级 SHA256 一致，127/127 命令共有，argKeys 0 不一致。**因此 win invoke 面是第一方 win 字节证据，非 mac 外推。**

**Gate**: owner-gate ADDITIVE — gate-report `windows-owner-closeout-gate-report.json` owner = <audit-session> (<workstation>)；本轮**不覆盖** canonical leaf 结论也不动既有 `dim1_shared_ccf_link`，只**追加** `dim1_win_first_party_ccf` 平行字段（本机 lane 自产证据的消费侧结论更新）。WIN-FRONTEND-CCF DISTILLED = 首写无碰撞。

**核心结论**：
1. **dim1 从"声明"→"字节证据"**：`<audit-session> 用 mac thin shared bundle"声明"闭的 13 条，本轮用 win-PE 本体 dump（字节证明 win==mac bundle）坐实为第一方 win 证据。≈20 个之前标 frontend_lane_gap / no_frontend_ccf / not_closed_windows 的命令 dim1 现用真 win CCF 闭，零外推。
2. **dim1 闭 ≠ 升 readyToImplement**：差 dim6（source archive acceptance，实现侧，逆向范围外）。≈20 命令 dims 1-5 闭后统一停 strictImplementationUse。
3. **唯一 tier 升级 = relay 3 个 HTTP-terminal**（见下表）。

### Relay 3 HTTP-terminal — 唯一应升 strict→readyToImplement

| cmd | 之前 dim1 | win CCF 第一方证据 | 判定 |
|---|---|---|---|
| test_relay_provider | not_closed_windows | useMutation.mutationFn @ use-relay-providers-BNphfsn5.js wrapper=i argKeys=[providerId] | **strict→readyToImplement**（证据最硬） |
| test_relay_draft | not_closed_windows | useMutation.mutationFn @ use-relay-providers-BNphfsn5.js wrapper=i argKeys=[input] | **strict→readyToImplement**（证据最硬） |
| fetch_relay_models_draft | not_closed_windows | wrapperCall @ relay-page-CljGSoid.js wrapper=Le argKeys=[input] + i18n relay.form.fetchModels.failed/empty/success | **strict→readyToImplement**（invoke+组件+i18n，onClick 未解析但 surface 坐实） |

依据：tier-matrix（`audits/windows-1.0.9-relay/data/tier-matrix.json`）三者 
ot_ready_reason` 明确"唯一剩余天花板 = dim1 frontend CCF (not_closed_windows)，需 real frontend UI-trigger CCF，doNotInferWindowsFromMacOS"。dim2-6 全闭 + HTTP-terminal 天花板已 lift（<audit-session> win UI-trigger CCF 闭掉这最后一道门。relay 另 15 个本就 readyToImplement（dim1=product_decision），win CCF 仅加固，不改 tier。

### theme dim1 第一方复核（SoT 偏差）

win 前端 dump grep `set_app_theme`/`set_theme` = 0 hits。`cmd_set_app_theme_coroutine`(dim1=js_invoke_setTheme) 与 `cmd_set_theme`(dim1=shared_bundle_ccf) 的 dim1 依据在 win 第一方站不住 → 建议复核（theme 或由 source archive 自前端处理 / 走 computed-field 分发，CCF 不可恢复）。非阻断：两命令 dims 2-5 闭，停 strictImplementationUse；dim1 建议改标 win_first_party_unconfirmed。

### backend-orphan 6 个第一方复核

execute_proxy_tools / rollback_threads_for_router / data_store_identifiers / data_store_remove / append_assistant_and_tool_results / mystery_unlock —— win 第一方 ipc-contracts(127) 全 0 hits，确认设计上无前端调用，停 strictImplementationUse 是正确终态，非 dim1 缺口。

**Verdict**: **win dim1 product gap 清掉。** 逆向侧 win dim1 闭合完成（第一方 win CCF，零外推）；relay 3 HTTP-terminal 应升 readyToImplement；残余 strict 卡的是 dim6（source archive 实现侧），非 dim1。真 dim1 缺口（前端有 invoke + 后端没逆）= 0。

### Remaining known schema notes (not noncompliant, documented)

- plugins x2: task-plan.json retains old `restoration.cm.task_plan.v1` schema (empty/stale pre-consumer-gate artifact). The authoritative consumer-gate document is consumer-gate.json with correct schema. task-plan.json is not the gate document for this bundle family and need not be corrected unless a consumer-gate schema migration is run across all bundles.
- mcp x2 + sessions-analytics x2: task-plan.json uses `restoration.cm.reverse.module_task_plan.v1` (module-level legacy schema with full `restoration.cm.reverse.` prefix). This is not one of the wrong strings targeted by l2 schema correction (`module_task_plan.v1` bare / `task_plan.v1` bare / `audit.task_plan.v1`). Content is correct; schema label is a legacy variant, not a defect.
